        -- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_3
        local v27 = p25:FindFirstChild("HealFlask")
        if p26 == 1 then
            if v27 then
                v27.Cork.Transparency = 1
                v_u_6.EffectToClient("SpawnSound", v_u_9.CorkOpen, p25.HumanoidRootPart, true)
                return
            end
        else
            if p26 == 2 then
                v_u_6.EffectToClient("SpawnSound", v_u_9.FlaskDrink, p25.HumanoidRootPart, true)
                return
            end
            if p26 == 3 then
                if v27 then
                    v27.Liquid.Transparency = 1
                end
                local v28 = p25:FindFirstChild("Buildups")
                if p25:FindFirstChild("RotProc") then
                    p25:FindFirstChild("RotProc"):Destroy()
                end
                if v28 then
                    local v29 = v28.Poison
                    v29.Value = v29.Value - 10
                    local v30 = v28.Rot
                    v30.Value = v30.Value - 10
                end
                v_u_6.EffectToClient("CharacterFX", p25, v_u_8.FlaskUse.HealFX, 2.5)
                v_u_3.HealthAdd(p25, p25.Humanoid.MaxHealth * 0.15)
            end
        end
    end,
    ["AttackEndFunction"] = function(p31)
        -- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_1
        v_u_3.ModelHandler(p31, v_u_1.Assets.HealFlask, false)
    end,
    ["DisruptFunction"] = function(p32)
        -- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_1
        v_u_3.ModelHandler(p32, v_u_1.Assets.HealFlask, false)
    end
}

        local v56 = p53:FindFirstChild("ShurikenBundle")
